              <h3 class="mod-slideshow-title">
                  <a href="https://www.reuters.com/news/picture/giving-birth-in-the-time-of-covid-19-idUSRTX7GF0Z">
                      Giving birth in the time of COVID-19</a>
              </h3>

    if (mostPopularSlideshow.length != 0) {
        ssCnt = mostPopularSlideshow[0].pages.length;

        function createSSTrending(ss) {
            var ssObj = mostPopularSlideshow[0];
            var ssRank = ss + 1;
            var ssLink = ssObj.pages[ss].path;
 var articleId =null;
if(ssLink.includes('='))
articleId = ssLink.substring(ssLink.indexOf('=') + 1);
else
articleId = ssLink.substring(ssLink.lastIndexOf('-id') + 3);
if(!articleId)
return;
            var chartbeatURL = '/assets/jsonArticle?isSlideshow=true&articleId=' + articleId;
            $("#most-popular ul").append('<li id="ssTrending-'+ssRank+'"><div class="most-popular-title"><div class="most-popular-img photo-thumb"><div class="slideshowOverlay"></div><a href="https://www.'+ssLink+'"></a></div><a href="https://www.'+ssLink+'" class="photo-title"></a></div></li>');
            $.getJSON(chartbeatURL, function (ssPhoto) {
                var ssTitle = ssPhoto.headline;
                var ssIMG = ssPhoto.image[0].url;

                if ($('#ssTrending-' + ssRank + ' img').height() > $('#ssTrending-' + ssRank + ' img').width()) {
                    $('#ssTrending-' + ssRank + ' .most-popular-img').addClass('photo-portrait')
                }
            });
        }

            createSSTrending(ssNum);
        }
